Types of costumes available: sport, casual, working, evening and night.\r\n\r\nThe goal of the game - in exchange for earned points purchase all available items for all available rooms and for the Backyard. And purchase all available toys.\r\n\r\nEgg Hunt.\r\nAnother goal is to hunt, find, collect and complete the collection of mini trophy creatures. You need to look for eggs, hunt, crack and hatch and finally own creatures which are inside the eggs. The eggs can be found randomly in different game locations. Need to wait after each crack in order to proceed with the following crack. The egg will be hatched after 3 cracks. The egg which was cracked once can be found in the same location.\r\n\r\nKarma represents your overall game progress and player experience.\r\n\r\n****\r\nThe girl will respond to the sounds of click on the Main screen.
